[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-      k = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-      n += [0m[1;35mscpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout, param, tmp, k[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+      k = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmantbuf, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmantbuf[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, mantissa, pr, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
